          <div class="content clearfix">

             <div class="flexslider optionset-default" id="flexslider-1">
              <ul class="slides">
               <li>
                <div class="views-field views-field-nothing">
                 <span class="field-content">
                  <a href="https://www.nspe.org/resources/pe-magazine/may-2018/engineering-difference">
                   <img alt="" height="356" src="https://www.nspe.org/sites/default/files/styles/slideshow/public/Cover_PEMag_May-June_homepage420px_0.jpg?itok=cQS5HohH" typeof="foaf:Image" width="420"/>

                <div class="views-field views-field-title">
                 <span class="field-content">
                  <a href="https://www.nspe.org/resources/pe-magazine/may-2018/engineering-difference">
                   Engineering a Difference
                  </a>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="views-field views-field-body">
                 <div class="field-content">
                  <p>
                   Young engineers want to make a positive impact both in and beyond their day-to-day work. Companies that grasp this perspective will earn these workers’ attention and loyalty.
                  </p>
                 </div>
                </div>
                <div class="views-field views-field-nothing-1">
                 <div class="field-content views-field-learn-more">

               </li>
